shared_focus = {
	id = ENG_the_prime_minister_speaks
	icon = GFX_ENG_the_prime_minister_speaks
	cost = 2
	prerequisite = {
		focus = ENG_tick_tack_tick_tack
	}
	mutually_exclusive = {
		focus = ENG_whole_state_under_there
	}
	relative_position_id = ENG_tick_tack_tick_tack
	x = -2
	y = 1
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ENG_the_prime_minister_speaks"
		custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_the_prime_minister_speaks_tt
		country_event = { id = ENG_intro.2 }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
				set_variable = { ENG_FutureSpeechSafetyMeter = 100 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = ENG_intro.13 days = 3 }
				set_variable = { ENG_FutureSpeechSafetyMeter = 40 }
				set_variable = { ENG_FutureSpeechSafetyMeter_Periodic = -10 }
			}
			set_variable = { ENG_Collab_Guns = 500 }
			set_country_flag = ENG_Player_Collab
			set_country_flag = ENG_GoogleMaps_Enabled
			country_event = { id = ENG_ForShip.18 days = 15 }
		}
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = ENG_the_kings_speech
	icon = GFX_ENG_the_kings_speech
	cost = 2
	prerequisite = {
		focus = ENG_keeping_ahead
		focus = ENG_writing_on_the_walls
	}
	relative_position_id = ENG_tick_tack_tick_tack
	x = 0
	y = 6
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ENG_the_kings_speech"
		custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_the_kings_speech_tt
		set_variable = { ENG_focus_id = 0 }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ENG_Player_Collab
				}
				country_event = { id = ENG_intro.11 }
				activate_mission = ENG_HMMLR_focus_mis
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ENG_Player_HMMLR
				}
				country_event = { id = ENG_intro.12 }
				activate_mission = ENG_Collab_focus_mis
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ENG_flavor.49
				days = 50
			}
			set_country_flag = ENG_GoogleMaps_ActiveDecisions
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { is_demilitarized_zone = no }
				ENG_GoogleMaps_Math = yes
			}
			set_country_flag = ENG_KingsSpeech_Over
		}
	}
}

	id = ENG_edwards_round_table
	icon = GFX_ENG_what_to_say
	cost = 1
	x = 0
	y = 0
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ENG_edwards_round_table"
		country_event = {
			id = ENG_collab_precw.1
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = ENG_Own_Peoples_Hate
			add_idea = ENG_Own_Peoples_Hate_2
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ENG_flavor.34
				days = 45
			}
			country_event = {
				id = preECW_HMMLR.1
				days = 45
			}
			country_event = {
				id = preECW_HMMLR.2
				days = 60
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = FEN_a_nation_reborn
	icon = GFX_ENG_Onwards_to_Democracy
	cost = 1

		focus = FEN_prepared_for_the_future
	}

		focus = FEN_the_english_phoenix
	}
	relative_position_id = FEN_a_forgotten_word_england
	x = 0
	y = 9
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus FEN_a_nation_reborn"
		# custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_reconstruction_election_tt
		# 
		TNO_improve_refugees_policy_effectiveness_med = yes
		#FEN_decrease_hunger = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = FEN_a_nation_reborn_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			FEN_a_nation_reborn = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_game_rule = { rule = HMMLR_IDEOLOGY_ROUTE option = HMMLR_IDEOLOGY_ROUTE_SOCCON } }
			every_owned_state = {
				set_variable = { TNO_Britain_ElectionSeason_AP_v = 50 }
				set_variable = { TNO_Britain_ElectionSeason_AP_pi = 12 }
				TNO_Britain_ElectionSeason_AddPop_InState = yes
				custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_ParliamentMechanic_Party_Support_12_add
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_game_rule = { rule = HMMLR_IDEOLOGY_ROUTE option = HMMLR_IDEOLOGY_ROUTE_LIBSOC } }
			every_owned_state = {
			set_variable = { TNO_Britain_ElectionSeason_AP_v = 50 }
			set_variable = { TNO_Britain_ElectionSeason_AP_pi = 14 }
			TNO_Britain_ElectionSeason_AddPop_InState = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_ParliamentMechanic_Party_Support_14_add
			}
		}
	}
}

				has_idea = FEN_NDL_a_better_engine
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = FEN_NDL_a_better_engine
				add_idea = FEN_NDL_better_engines2
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = FEN_NDL_better_engines
		}
	}
}

						target = ENG
						modifier = ENG_international_brotherhood
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_international_brotherhood.tt
	}
